const filterInfo1 = await page.evaluate(() => {
  const nodes = [...document.querySelectorAll('input[type="checkbox"], label, button, a')];
  return nodes.map((el,i)=>({i, tag:el.tagName, text:(el.innerText||el.textContent||el.getAttribute('aria-label')||'').trim().replace(/\s+/g,' ').slice(0,80), id:el.id, name:el.getAttribute('name'), value:el.getAttribute('value'), href:el.getAttribute('href'), checked:el.checked, cls:el.className})).filter(x=>/\$|rating|star|5|average|price|\$5|\$10|\$15/i.test(x.text+x.name+x.value+x.id));
});

<request>
const matches7 = await page.evaluate(() => {
  const cards = [...document.querySelectorAll('li')];
  const out = [];
  for (const li of cards) {
    const links = [...li.querySelectorAll('a[href*="/p/"]')];
    const nameLink = links.find(a => (a.innerText || '').trim().length > 10);
    if (!nameLink) continue;
    const name = nameLink.innerText.trim().replace(/\s+/g,' ');
    const text = li.innerText.trim().replace(/\s+/g,' ');
    const priceMatches = [...text.matchAll(/\$(\d+(?:\.\d{2})?)/g)].map(m => Number(m[1]));
    const salePrice = priceMatches[0];
    const reviewText = [...links].map(a => (a.innerText||'').trim()).find(t => /^\d+(,\d+)?$/.test(t));
    if (salePrice && salePrice < 20) {
      out.push({name, price: `$${salePrice.toFixed(salePrice % 1 ? 2 : 0)}`, reviews: reviewText || '', href: new URL(nameLink.getAttribute('href'), location.origin).href, cardText:text});
    }
  }
  // de-dupe by href
  return [...new Map(out.map(x => [x.href, x])).values()];
});
console.log(JSON.stringify(matches7, null, 2));
</request>

[46] tool_call: repl("Scraping 5-star search results")
<request>
await page.goto('https://www.jcpenney.com/s?searchTerm=boys+shoes&average_rating=5+rating');
const s18 = await snapshot(page);
console.log('URL:', page.url());
console.log(s18.tree);
const products10 = await page.evaluate(() => {
  const anchors = [...document.querySelectorAll('a[href*="/p/"]')];
  const rows = [];
  for (const a of anchors) {
    const text = (a.innerText || a.textContent || '').trim().replace(/\s+/g, ' ');
    const href = a.href;
    // product cards often have a text-only link and the closest list item contains price/review text
    const container = a.closest('li') || a.closest('[data-testid*="product" i]') || a.closest('[class*="product" i]') || a.parentElement;
    const cardText = (container?.innerText || text).trim().replace(/\s+/g, ' ');
    rows.push({text, href, cardText});
  }
  const byHref = new Map();
  for (const r of rows) {
    const existing = byHref.get(r.href);
    const score = (r.text.length > 15 ? 2 : 0) + (r.cardText.includes('$') ? 2 : 0) + r.cardText.length/1000;
    if (!existing || score > existing.score) byHref.set(r.href, {...r, score});
  }
  const out = [];
  for (const r of byHref.values()) {
    const txt = r.cardText || r.text;
    const priceMatch = txt.match(/\$(\d+(?:\.\d{2})?)(?!\d)/);
    const price = priceMatch ? Number(priceMatch[1]) : null;
    const name = (r.text && !/^\d+$/.test(r.text) && !r.text.includes('$') ? r.text : txt.split(/\s+(?:LIMITED TIME SPECIAL!|BUY 1 GET|\$)/)[0]).trim();
    const reviewMatch = txt.match(/(?:\$\d+(?:\.\d{2})?[^\d]*)(\d+(?:,\d+)?)$/);
    out.push({name, price, href:r.href, cardText:txt});
  }
  return out.filter(p => p.price !== null).filter(p => p.price < 20);
});
